***неизбежный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неизбежный.html>неизбе́жный</a> (4617)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неизбежный.html>неизбе́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neizbéžnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неизбе́жнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неизбе́жней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>inevitable, unavoidable, inescapable</li>
<li>usual, commonly used</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изведать.html>изве́данный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvédannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неизведанный.html>неизве́данный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neizvédannyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неизве́даннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неизве́данней</b>)
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>дан</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>мый</b>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>мый</b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вки</a>: <b>не-из-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-мер-</b>; суффикс: <b>-им</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***неимение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неимение.html>неиме́ние</a> (22906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неимение.html>неиме́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neiménije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неимение.html>неиме́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неимение.html>неиме́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неимение.html>неиме́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>absence, lack, want</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ме́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неиссякаемый.html>неиссяка́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neissjakájemyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неиссяка́емее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неиссяка́емей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>never running dry <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a spring or well</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inexhaustible</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>и́с<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тов<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ство<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>

<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истовый.html>и́стовый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ístovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неистовый.html>неи́стовые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:аплодисменты.html>аплодисме́нты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neístovyje</b> aplodisménty</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>thundering/rapturous</b> applause</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нейтрализовать.html>нейтрализова́ть</a> (14607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неказистый.html>некази́стый</a> (18696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">каз(а́ться)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaz(átʹsja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́стый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***некий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:некий.html>некий</a> (1115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некий.html>не́кий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nékij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a certain, certain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некий.html>не́кий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гражданин.html>граждани́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:распространить.html>распространи́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слух.html>слух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nékij</b> graždanín rasprostraníl slux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A certain citizen spread a rumor.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:некий.html>не́кая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nékaja</b> žénščina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a certain woman</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>some</li></ol>
